Overview Notes: A high fasting insulin may indicate insulin resistance and if not managed may lead to Diabetes. Follow a low carbohydrate and sugar free diet, increase your exercise levels as able to and lose weight specifically around your abdomen. Please recheck level in 6 weeks.
Comment Key: ClinicalExamComment
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: High fasting insulin but normal fasting glucose. Low DHEA

Women's Health Recommendations:
